  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b79a443d-aaa3-47de-8961-74e269d53e88'
      });
    }

<div id="review_838807472" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/838807472" />
    <a title="Rachel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11629051-rachel"><img alt="Rachel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389832057p2/11629051.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/838807472?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel" href="/user/show/11629051-rachel">Rachel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11629051-rachel?shelf=kindle-lending-shelf">kindle-lending-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11629051-rachel?shelf=just-crap">just-crap</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer838807472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer498086525710247468">I GIVE! I SURRENDER! I can't take it anymore!<br/><br/>UGH! Okay here's a list:<br/><br/>1. The writing is juvenile. Seriously.<br/><br/>2. The MC cries over everything, slut shames, and acts ridiculous. She feels like a teenager and is supposed to be 28. Also, she's supposed to have lost her daughter, and I just don't feel that at all. It feels like a plot device, which is all it is.<br/><br/>3. Nik is a woman with a penis. Enough said.<br/><br/>4. This quote: <b>"When Mimi told me she was bi-sexual I was shocked. She didn't look the type. Don't </b></span>
  <span id="freeText498086525710247468" style="display:none">I GIVE! I SURRENDER! I can't take it anymore!<br /><br />UGH! Okay here's a list:<br /><br />1. The writing is juvenile. Seriously.<br /><br />2. The MC cries over everything, slut shames, and acts ridiculous. She feels like a teenager and is supposed to be 28. Also, she's supposed to have lost her daughter, and I just don't feel that at all. It feels like a plot device, which is all it is.<br /><br />3. Nik is a woman with a penis. Enough said.<br /><br />4. This quote: <b>"When Mimi told me she was bi-sexual I was shocked. She didn't look the type. Don't get me wrong, I'm good with it. I love love. In all shapes and forms. And I love Mimi as a lesbian. She becomes a vixen." </b><br /><br />I can't... I can't even... Oh my god. Seriously, editor! Complete sentences and proper punctuation are important. And wow... I've never been so insulted by a romance novel. I can't even being to point out everything that is wrong with that paragraph.<br /><br />5. The entire thing with Sissy was atrocious. One, I feel bad for her. Two, the scene in the club was just embarrassing. You're acting like a child, let him handle his shit. Three, stop using women as plot devices! Ugh! The whole thing just made me feel dirty.<br /><br />6. The ridiculous virginal nature of the MC. Another near virginal, pure girl with the slutty man. The guy who sleeps around doesn't respect women who sleep around. Really? Must we keep pushing this stereotype? Better keep you legs together honey or no good man will want you! <br /><br />One of the worst books I've read all year.</span>
  <a data-text-id="498086525710247468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_675511211" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/675511211" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/675511211?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer675511211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1467303814471543360"><b>4.5 Lets Be Friends stars!!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/cad5d151-a524-415b-bffe-d33d7eeed505_zpsc557c664.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862707.jpg' alt=' photo cad5d151-a524-415b-bffe-d33d7eeed505_zpsc557c664.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After all the intense, emotional books I’ve read lately, I needed a pick me up- a feel good read... this had some touching and emotional moments, but overall it was hilarious, charming, sweet, sexy and EXACTLY what I needed! <br/><br/>Tina is a store owner in NYC. After a heartbreaking few years in California, she wanted a fresh start. Tina is funny, sweet, loving and kind. A fabulous heroine. <br/><br/>Nik owns the club across the street from Tina’s store. He is oh so sexy! Tina no</span>
  <span id="freeText1467303814471543360" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Lets Be Friends stars!!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/cad5d151-a524-415b-bffe-d33d7eeed505_zpsc557c664.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862707.jpg" alt=" photo cad5d151-a524-415b-bffe-d33d7eeed505_zpsc557c664.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After all the intense, emotional books I’ve read lately, I needed a pick me up- a feel good read... this had some touching and emotional moments, but overall it was hilarious, charming, sweet, sexy and EXACTLY what I needed! <br><br>Tina is a store owner in NYC. After a heartbreaking few years in California, she wanted a fresh start. Tina is funny, sweet, loving and kind. A fabulous heroine. <br><br>Nik owns the club across the street from Tina’s store. He is oh so sexy! Tina notices him taking smoke breaks everyday. He is gorgeous, but she never see’s him smile. She decides to send him something anonymously to change that. It’s just the type of person she is. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/2c6b1b49-1764-4cc2-bb2e-a01882f20c75_zps7cc19827.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862708.jpg" alt=" photo 2c6b1b49-1764-4cc2-bb2e-a01882f20c75_zps7cc19827.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tina and Nick are very different, but they have one thing in common. Neither one has any interest in a relationship whatsoever. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>HER:<br> “I don’t do relationships. I’m twenty-eight years old and have only been in one relationship. It was good in the beginning. It totally sucked at the end. Never again.”<br><br>  HIM:<br> “I don’t have relationships or girlfriends. I have fuck buddies. Because I fuck. Often. I most definitely don’t make love. I might not screw all the time but even slow screwing is just screwing.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Nik figures out fairly quickly Tina was the one who sent him the note and candy. At first, it makes him a little nervous. What kind of woman send a man candy? Does she have ulterior motives? She quickly does something that throws Nik off... she puts him in the friend zone, somewhere he has never been before. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/FriendZone-yep_zps6afe9855.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862709.jpg" alt=" photo FriendZone-yep_zps6afe9855.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“So we can be friends, right?”</i>
</b><br><i>Wait, what?<br>I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.<br>Did I..? Did I just get Friend-zoned?</i><br><br>Tina and Nik have the funnest and sweetest friendship. I loved watching it grow. They were both just too funny, lovable characters. Not only were Tina and Nik great, but the secondary characters were equally fantastic. I especially loved Nik’s brother, Max. Nik finds out soon enough that Tina is unlike any other woman he has ever known. She is kind, giving, caring, funny. He starts to develop real feelings for her, but they are just friends... he can’t have those. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I want to kiss her and taste every inch of her gorgeous body. I want to hold her while she sleeps. I want to protect her from everything thats bad in the world. I want her to need me. But we’re friends. And friends don’t do shit like that.</blockquote>
</i> Tina is slowly falling for Nik, she doesn’t want to admit it. She doesn’t think she can take that risk again, and with Nik of all people.. she has come to love him, lean on him, and she values his friendship. She doesn’t want to ruin that. Someone from Nik’s past comes into the picture, gives Tina some trouble. It gives Nik the motivation he needs to get out of the friend zone. For the first time in his life, he wants something real, with Tina.<br><i>
  <blockquote>‘I thought I needed a woman like you. Turns out, I just needed you.’</blockquote>
</i><br>Tina has had her walls up for the last few years. If anyone can break through them, it’s Nik. She loves him and she is willing to try...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ff2a253b-24ed-4bb9-bbaf-8a9ca8cbeed0_zps6a929469.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862710.jpg" alt=" photo ff2a253b-24ed-4bb9-bbaf-8a9ca8cbeed0_zps6a929469.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/56048d4f-65a0-4d0b-93c5-3cd4f25a4b65_zps37720902.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862711.jpg" alt=" photo 56048d4f-65a0-4d0b-93c5-3cd4f25a4b65_zps37720902.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is a little extra drama towards the end, but overall, I really enjoyed this book. It was so entertaining. Laugh out loud good. The main characters were both just too funny. I loved their inner monologues and some of the things that came out of their mouths just cracked me up! <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’re pussy whipped.”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <i>I claim,</i>
  <i>
    <b> “I can’t be pussy whipped. I haven’t even had the pussy to be whipped!”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <i>Take that, Ghost! Oh, wait…<br>He chuckles, </i>
  <b>
    <i>“That’s even worse, bro.”</i>
  </b>
  <br>
  <i>Fuck me, it totally is.</i>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Can everyone shut the fuck up?”</i></b><br><i>My dad gasps and says,</i><br><i><b>“Valentina, you no be rude you friends like that!”</b></i> <i>I nod my head in agreement and try again,</i><br><b><i>“Can everyone please shut the fuck up?”</i></b>
</blockquote><br>If you are looking for a sweet, funny, romantic, feel good love story, pick this one up! It is the perfect light read, with just enough emotion. A beautiful ending. Looking forward to the second book in the series (Nat and Ghost) and here’s hoping Max gets his own story! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d50130e2-d136-478c-bbc3-894712bddbfa_zpsd9c5d519.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430314i/862712.jpg" alt=" photo d50130e2-d136-478c-bbc3-894712bddbfa_zpsd9c5d519.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>‘You’re it. The one. The start. The finish. You are how my story ends.’</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1467303814471543360" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_602680727" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/602680727" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/602680727?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301943234" href="/book/show/17566523-friend-zoned">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=addicted-to-this-author">addicted-to-this-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer602680727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15194622177660796675"><b>4 STARS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419459i/831596._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419459i/831597._SX540_.jpg' width='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Did I ... ? Did I just get friend - zoned?"</b>
</i><br/><br/>There was plenty to love about 'Friend zoned' in fact for the first 55% I had that feeling of 'best book of 2013', but unfortunately this went a little south around the 60% mark and I felt a little conflicted about my initial love for the book, I think my main issue was the differing story lines, was I reading a light weight romance, or action suspense story? Nevertheless I would definitely recommend 'Friend -Zoned' to those that love chick</span>
  <span id="freeText15194622177660796675" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419459i/831596._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419459i/831597._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"Did I ... ? Did I just get friend - zoned?"</b>
</i><br><br>There was plenty to love about 'Friend zoned' in fact for the first 55% I had that feeling of 'best book of 2013', but unfortunately this went a little south around the 60% mark and I felt a little conflicted about my initial love for the book, I think my main issue was the differing story lines, was I reading a light weight romance, or action suspense story? Nevertheless I would definitely recommend 'Friend -Zoned' to those that love chick lit and a dose of funny humour. For the most part this book was laced with 5 star moments, but for me it also lacked that certain all round 'love every page' factor so it ended up with a healthy 4 stars from me. <br><br><b>What's its all about?</b><br>Nikolai 'Nik' Leokov is the owner of popular club the white rabbit, nik is a typical 'man about town' with his life in order and a booming business. The only time this man thinks about having a woman in his life is when he has a pretty lady in between his sheets. So with no time for a serious relationship he can't possibly be prepared for when local business woman Valentina Tomic explodes into his life and heart with nothing more than an offer of friendship, but the course of love never does run smooth when there is secrets of the past, failure to commit and a host of miscommunication. Nik and Tina are the prefect friends and completely enjoyable characters, they hold an undeniable attraction for each other that may just take them out of the 'friend zone'.<br><br><b>Meet the characters ...</b><br>Nikolai Leokov is a readers dream, handsome, well dressed, the best kind of family man and to top it off he also boasts some yummy tattoos. This author went straight for the heart when she thought up this hero. A dual point of view meant we didn't miss any of the action from Nik and I was convinced by this character. Nik is a bucketful of sweet, sexy and straight up protective of those he loves, every girl needs a Nikolai Leotov.<br><br>Valentina 'Tina' Tomic is a character I will not be forgetting in a hurry she was dorky, geeky, gorgeous and had a sense of humour to rival most of the heroines I've ever read about. I loved her inner dialogue and amusing Tina isms yes, she amused me from page one and I'm now on the hunt for a friend just like her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419460i/831598._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love ...</b><br>'Friend - Zoned' captured friendship and family perfectly, I loved how the characters slotted into each others lives. Tina and her girl friends were probably what I enjoyed most about the story I loved their witty banter and humorous conversations, There was never a dull moment throughout the book, it was entertaining and it certainly caused a few chuckles in its funnier moments. Nik and his family are a crowd pleaser, I've mentioned before in reviews that I love when a series links it's characters and if I get to see more of Max, Ghost, Trick and all the others then I will be one happy reader. Surprisingly for such a funny, cute story it also had depth and moments of sadness that I'm not sure flowed with the rest of the story but I could understand what the author was trying to achieve I just didn't agree with some of the conflicting story lines, however it does prove that this author is able to cover a range of topics and write them well. 'Friend - Zoned' is a story with a laugh a minute I'm so glad that I was recommended this story by my good reads girls, I'm glad I one clicked this book, no regrets from me.<br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>I feel a little disappointed that I was unable to crown this book 'best read of 2013' there was shining moments that I truly thought meant id found myself the perfect book, but sadly it didn't hold up my five star fixation. But I don't want to sound negative this was an enjoyable read for me. I can't wait to delve into book two, for two reasons, firstly I have a buddy read lined up with my stateside bestie friend, Christy and secondly because the author left me excited to learn more about her interesting characters. 'Friend - Zoned' is a witty, romantic story that captured friendship and true love at its best, I know that this will be a winner for most ... Go grab it readers, kisses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419460i/831599._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15194622177660796675" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

It's hilarious and practically delightful. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora' title='Belle Aurora' rel='nofollow noopener'>Belle Aurora</a> laced this book with humor and pure entertainment that readers will surely laugh out loud.<br/><br/>This book is actually a decent NA read. But while I didn't hate it or anything, it left quite me unsatisfied because I was expecting something different. I loved the story. The plot was simple and interesting but I wasn't convince</span>
  <span id="freeText10976421248096455291" style="display:none">(Buddyread with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1462240217?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Allie.</a> Check out her full review. :))<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17948485.Friend_Zoned__Friend_Zoned___1_" title="Friend-Zoned (Friend-Zoned, #1) by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Friend-Zoned</a> is one of those books you would gladly read for pleasure. It's hilarious and practically delightful. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora" title="Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Belle Aurora</a> laced this book with humor and pure entertainment that readers will surely laugh out loud.<br><br>This book is actually a decent NA read. But while I didn't hate it or anything, it left quite me unsatisfied because I was expecting something different. I loved the story. The plot was simple and interesting but I wasn't convinced with the delivery especially because of its slow pacing that dragged most parts of the book.<br><br>I also had an issue with the main character <b>Tina</b> who acted so childish despite her mature age. But it doesn't mean I was annoyed with her. It's just that I'm weirded out by her personality. In the end though, I warmed up to her because of what happened to her in the past. It was in the last few chapters of the book that I totally empathized with her.<br><br><b>Nik</b>, on the other hand, was a great character. He's a bit cliché but he's one of the most likable of people to read about. He's a typical rich casanova but he's sweet and very passionate when he seriously falls for someone. I definitely swooned a lot with the way he cared for Tina. :)<br><br>All in all, this book is an enjoyable read but for me, it's nothing extraordinary. I'm not closing my doors for this author though because I really want to read her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18071296.Willing_Captive" title="Willing Captive by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Willing Captive</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26827731.Lev__Shot_Callers___1_" title="Lev (Shot Callers, #1) by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Lev</a> which are highly recommended by friends. :)<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446078794i/16744105.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>

<div id="review_625019264" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/625019264" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/625019264?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=more-than-friends">more-than-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer625019264" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6737475998298555938">I tend to love friends to lovers stories. They're so honest and relatable if ever you found yourself in a similar situation from times past.<br/><br/>But, I didn't love this one.<br/><br/>To be honest, I actually contemplated shelving it about 65% in. Why?<br/><br/>Tina. It was all Tina's fault, hehe!<br/><br/>The plot was cool. The secondary characters were cool, especially Ghost. There was just something about him. I found myself wanting to know his story and luckily book #2 will be about him and Natalie--if I decide to read it-- Bu</span>
  <span id="freeText6737475998298555938" style="display:none">I tend to love friends to lovers stories. They're so honest and relatable if ever you found yourself in a similar situation from times past.<br /><br />But, I didn't love this one.<br /><br />To be honest, I actually contemplated shelving it about 65% in. Why?<br /><br />Tina. It was all Tina's fault, hehe!<br /><br />The plot was cool. The secondary characters were cool, especially Ghost. There was just something about him. I found myself wanting to know his story and luckily book #2 will be about him and Natalie--if I decide to read it-- But back to Tina.<br /><br />She irritated THE HELL out of me, no joke! She was a little too sacharrine, a little too sweet, a little too play-the-deer-in-headlights-type with her widened eyes, and *GASP!* reactions. Just as an example, no spoiler here: She sees a weapon--not in use but described as for safety reasons-- and when asked to hold it, she tucks her arms under her armpits and exclaims in a feirce whisper, " I don't want my prints on it!!" REALLY??!! is that supposed to be funny? cute? I'm thinking RIDICULOUS.<br /><br />This is one of an endless number of examples why she bugged me. I kept trying to figure out if her characterization was meant to be goofy-cute or naive but smart. But, to me it came across as trying too hard and failing miserably. She often spoke in EXCLAMATIONS!!!!! all the time!!! And she made comments that were annoying at best. <br /><br />There were also many scenes that I thought if happened in real life, there would be a very different reaction to them. Again for examples sake, no spoiler: Deciding to scope out someones house without asking and then entering a room and helping yourself to whatever's in there. REALLY?? do normal people do that? As a host I would find that rude and pretentious. But this is just me.<br /><br />Like I said, the story itself wasn't bad neither were the secondary characters but if the h is dragging down the book then I can't look past that and give more stars. I know a lot of people liked it very much and I can see why. It had it's funny moments and scenarios and Nik was yummy...so Yes, I can see why it was well recieved. But you can't love em' all and this unfortunately fell in the don't like category for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6737475998298555938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1951456237914429027">Yes I did finish this, because clearly miracles actually happen!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452720521i/17732620.jpg' width='250' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What the fuck did I just read, someone please explain to me how the fuck so many people gave this book 5 stars. The only reasoning I can come to is that they were drunk and on some really trippy drugs because this was just a whole load of stupid. <br/><br/>This heroine is supposed to be 28?! Really? I mean REALLY? I thought she was 12 because this bitch was the most immature character I have ever read about. I wanted to slap her so hard her w</span>
  <span id="freeText1951456237914429027" style="display:none">Yes I did finish this, because clearly miracles actually happen!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452720521i/17732620.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What the fuck did I just read, someone please explain to me how the fuck so many people gave this book 5 stars. The only reasoning I can come to is that they were drunk and on some really trippy drugs because this was just a whole load of stupid. <br><br>This heroine is supposed to be 28?! Really? Gawd!!!" </b> at the age of 28! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421171625ra/13333614.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Nik. That man must have spent his entire 35 years of life looking for his balls, because he was the biggest pussy I've ever come across. A big badass ex-gang member with a scary gun? Was it a Nerf gun and was the gang a Care Bears fan group? Granted he is slightly more mature than whatever her name was, but not by much. And he's supposed to be sexy?! Even his big dick didn't help his case and I can forgive a lot of issues for some man meat. <br><br>What actually surprised me the most was how they had time to fit any sex in what with ALL THE BLOODY CRYING. These women should have bought shares with Kleenex, they'd be minted by now if they had.<br><br>It wasn't like Sharknado were it's so bad it's good, NOPE it's just bad. <br><br>At this point I don't even give a shit about how harsh I've been. *SORRY - NOT SORRY!*<br><br>The only hope left is that the author wrote this when she was really young, only then could I slightly forgive the immaturity of the whole thing and attempt another book by her.<br><br>*Edit to say that I have read and really liked another book by this author, so there is hope*</span>

  <span id="freeText13303622337821068600" style="display:none">The amount of great reviews for this book is mind-boggling. <div id="review_596175488" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/596175488" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/596175488?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301943234" href="/book/show/17566523-friend-zoned">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=april-2013">april-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596175488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16746371787237577091"><b>Clap your hands, plastic lips and penis Tetris...</b> <br/><br/>None of which will make sense until you read <i>Friend-Zoned</i>, but I'm giddy. Slap your ass giddy! Hallelujah, amen a book that finally killed insta-love with sexual tension. A book that knows how to make us wait, tease us, draw it out, tickle our fancy. By the way "Fancy" is the name of my....never mind.<br/><br/>Sexual tension <i>is</i> the elixir of life, the nectar of the gods...a smooth shot of tequila!! My thirst has been quenched. Nik and Tina's sexually charg</span>
  <span id="freeText16746371787237577091" style="display:none"><b>Clap your hands, plastic lips and penis Tetris...</b> <br /><br />None of which will make sense until you read <i>Friend-Zoned</i>, but I'm giddy. Slap your ass giddy! Hallelujah, amen a book that finally killed insta-love with sexual tension. A book that knows how to make us wait, tease us, draw it out, tickle our fancy. By the way "Fancy" is the name of my....never mind.<br /><br />Sexual tension <i>is</i> the elixir of life, the nectar of the gods...a smooth shot of tequila!! My thirst has been quenched. Nik and Tina's sexually charged friendship was--is...it was just what I needed. <br /><br />I could not put this book down; it had the same addictive quality I find in many Kristen Ashley novels. You fall in love with the characters...<i>all</i> of the characters. Nik, Trick, Asher, Max...big soft hearts encased in hot alpha male bodies. I fell in love. <br /><br />This book was a big ball of everything; humor, sexual tension, friendship. Even parts that pulled at your heartstrings. It had everything from troubled pasts to Will Ferrel and the "sprinkler". I laughed out loud one minute and my heart clinched the next. We get our fun and our drama!! <br /><br />Those of you who like to wear your nitpickers.com shirts will definitely find flaws; a few editing mistakes, some plot holes. It wasn't perfect. It even had a few draggy bits where there should have been less internal monologue and more dialogue, but I didn't care. I was thoroughly, thoroughly entertained and I haven't felt that way in a long time. <br /><br />The author gives us drama, but manages to keep it light and fun. It's hilarious, touching, and full of action. My kind of trifecta! I wanted so much to be a character in this book and I can't wait for the next one.<br /><br />Belle Aurora is definitely one to keep your eye on!<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16746371787237577091" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2444049796" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2444049796?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2444049796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer963847964151908376">How ridiculous I am to think <i>Friend-Zoned</i> is a mafia book? I picked it up without reading the blurb just to set my mood for a romantic suspense and after several chapters, I was laughing out loud. Never would I've thought it's a romantic comedy and I actually had a good time reading this. <br/><br/><b>Valentina Tomic</b> is the owner of a clothing boutique called <i>Safira</i>. She's sassy, bold, bubbly and hilarious. Despite being immature, I can't help laughing on her shenanigans. I think it's her way of coping after</span>
  <span id="freeText963847964151908376" style="display:none">How ridiculous I am to think <i>Friend-Zoned</i> is a mafia book? I picked it up without reading the blurb just to set my mood for a romantic suspense and after several chapters, I was laughing out loud. Never would I've thought it's a romantic comedy and I actually had a good time reading this. <br /><br /><b>Valentina Tomic</b> is the owner of a clothing boutique called <i>Safira</i>. She's sassy, bold, bubbly and hilarious. Despite being immature, I can't help laughing on her shenanigans. I think it's her way of coping after an unfortunate event in the past. It's the reason she's been single for years. <br /><br />She notices an attractive but brooding man across her store. Tina befriends this guy by sending lip-shaped candies to cheer him up. Apparently, he is <b>Nikolai Leokov</b>, the owner of the <i>The White</i> which is a club across her store. <br /><br />Tina and Nik are obviously attracted to each other but both of them have issues as far as relationship goes. The friendship between them was solid and it's even more fruitful when they took it to the next level. They slowly opened up to each other and I find it really sweet. Tina is thoughtful, caring and loyal to her family and friends. These qualities made Nik fall in love with her. He's protective, sweet and selfless. Quite an alpha guy. <br /><br />This novel reminds me of <i>Wallbanger</i> with an organize crime group. Nik, Max, and Ghost are former gang members but they still have minor involvement outside the business. I love the humor and friendship here more. The secondary characters Max, Mimi, Ghost (he's by far my favorite!), Nat, Lola and Trick are great. I know I'm so late but I am excited to read their stories.</span>
  <a data-text-id="963847964151908376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText3932677617820604379" style="display:none"><b>"Why not go out on a limb? Isn't that where the fruit is?"</b><br /><br />A funny, not to mention SEXY, friends to lovers story gets me every damned time. Tina and Nik were so perfect together, from the moment she meets him by sending him candy wax lips in the hopes she'd finally see him smile until their eventual HEA.         rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer602457341" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11758975547024507813"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419427i/831469._SX540_.jpg' width='290' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Friend Zoned</i> brought out so many emotions in me. This book was quirky and funny, sad and tragic, action packed and exciting. <br/><br/>Tina Tomic is the owner of Safira clothing store. She left her life in California for a new start two years ago. While looking out her store window, she notices the gorgeous owner of The White Rabbit night club across the street Nikolai Leokov taking smoke breaks. <br/> <br/>Tina works with two great girls, Lola and Meems. Her best friend, Nan is expected to move in with her and st</span>
  <span id="freeText11758975547024507813" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419427i/831469._SX540_.jpg" width="290" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Friend Zoned</i> brought out so many emotions in me. This book was quirky and funny, sad and tragic, action packed and exciting. <br><br>Tina Tomic is the owner of Safira clothing store. She left her life in California for a new start two years ago. While looking out her store window, she notices the gorgeous owner of The White Rabbit night club across the street Nikolai Leokov taking smoke breaks. <br> <br>Tina works with two great girls, Lola and Meems. Her best friend, Nan is expected to move in with her and start working with her as well. Life is pretty good except for that gorgeous guy across the street’s frown. <br><br>It all started with a gift of a pair of wax lips with a card saying: <br><br><b>
  <i>”Smile sometime, handsome.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419427i/831470.jpg" width="200" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>When Nik receives his gift, he immediately sends for Tina to figure out her motives. He is pretty taken by her derriere and her quirkiness. Their conversation goes well until…<br><br><b>
  <i>”So we can be friends, right?”<br>Wait, what?<br>I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.<br>Did I…? Did I just get friend-zoned?”</i>
</b><br><br>The large cast of characters in this book were all well done and I’m guessing that they will receive books as well. Some were mysterious like Ghost, some were sweet and heart breaking like Max and some were just fun like Lola and Meems. <br><br>Tina’s friends and Nik’s friends become friends. They enjoy each other’s company and it’s a good time. Nik and Tina do lunches, hang out and the sexual tension is abundant!<br><br>Although Tina is a cupcake baking machine and a sweetheart she does harbor tremendous grief. The scene where the girls sing at the piano was a tough one. <br> <br>When these two get together and learn to trust it seems that all is well until…Omar. Well you see, Nik has family ties to a Russian-American gang and a crazy guy is smitten with Tina. Then there’s her ex who appears as well. Have no fear this book ends with a sweet hea.<br><br>Bella Aurora does a great job with this debut novel, it had a bit of everything! </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=sexy-suit-and-ties">sexy-suit-and-ties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=lol-funny">lol-funny</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer816434443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11459352722262914447"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4 Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389333788ra/8022157.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“So we can be friends, right?”<br/><br/><i>Wait, what?</i><br/>I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.<br/><i>Did I…? Did I just get Friend-zoned?</i><br/>I look over again to see Tina nodding vigorously and smiling brightly.<br/>Wow, this has never happened to me before.<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>This book was so awesome! It had a little bit of everything. I think it's the perfect book if you don't want a read that has over the top angst.</span>
  <span id="freeText11459352722262914447" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389333788ra/8022157.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“So we can be friends, right?”<br><br><i>Wait, what?</i><br>I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.<br><i>Did I…? Did I just get Friend-zoned?</i><br>I look over again to see Tina nodding vigorously and smiling brightly.<br>Wow, this has never happened to me before.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book was so awesome! It had a little bit of everything. I think it's the perfect book if you don't want a read that has over the top angst. It was humourous with such entertaining and lovable characters. And high levels of steam. Definitely one you should read after an emotionally draining book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389333788ra/8022158.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Nik and Tina do not do relationships. Nik, because he is simply not interested at the moment and can't trust women. Tina, because she was completely shattered in her previous relationship that she swore 'never again'. Tina notices Nik from across the street in her clothing store, Safira. He is always hanging around at the nightclub The White Rabbit during the day. There is one thing she notices about him. Yes, he is über smexy. But, he never smiles. So, she decides to send him candy and a note, and the rest is history. They become the bestest of 'friends'.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>I like that Tina is in my bed with me and we haven't had sex. It's more than that with her. I want to be her protector and the one who she comes to with her problems. She feels good against me. So soft and lush. I could get use to this. Contentment washes over me.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Tina was a really funny character. I've noticed that Bella Aurora loves giving her characters a 'crazy colourful' mind, full of funny and quirky banter. Which, I personally love. Tina was just like that. The random things that pop in to her head, and her random expressions made me chuckle. She was sweet, caring, and could bake the most delicious treats. She was independent, a tad bit crazy, goofy, and quite strong. A character who really complimented Nik's personality. She was awesome.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>I love this man. Actually love him. With all my heart. There's no denying it anymore. I feel safe with him. Whatever sadness I feel living my life is gone as soon as I see Nik. He makes the days' worth getting up for in the morning. My heart swells every time I see him shoot that dimple my way.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Nik is the owner of the nightclub she sees him in. When Tina bulldozes her way into his life, he didn't know what to think. He instantly thought "she wants a relationship, and might be after his money." But when she just wants to be friends, he can't believe. He is attracted to her. He knows this could be dangerous, and yet, he finds himself agreeing. Nik was the protector. He cares deeply about his loved oned and goes to any lengths for them. It was beautiful to see these two become friends, and later on, become lovers. Because this way, we get to see thier love grow for one another.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389333788ra/8022159.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The steam was super sexy!! I loved the build up in this book. I couldn't wait for them to get it on! ha! The sexual tension was just perfect. And when they got together, it was smoking hot!! Nik is one sexy beast!! Yowza!! Loved him!! So, it definitely didn't disappoint.<br><br>The supporting characters were just as wonderful! They were each crazy in their own way. A bunch of people that don't look like they would get along but do. They were all so funny and loud. I loved seeing the whole gang interact together. And Nik's niece CeeCee, stole my heart. She was such a sweetheart. Loved her!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You’re it. The one. The start. The finish. You are how my story ends.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>The book is light, with many funny moments. As well as a tiny bit of angst thrown in to keeps things entertaining. I loved the chemistry between all the characters. Some parts were a tad bit cheesy in my opinion but for the most part, very enjoyable. I loved getting to know the character's backgrounds. Some parts were also really sad. The ending was absolutely sweet!! I loved it! I recommend this book to people looking for a book that will lift up their spirits and leave them with a feel good feeling. I can't wait to read more of this series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11459352722262914447" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1533063081" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1533063081" />
    <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed"><img alt="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455042547p2/22911953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1533063081?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=books-they-make-you-read-in-hell">books-they-make-you-read-in-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=modern">modern</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1533063081" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16074802044241911349">I think I may have encephalitis, because I can't think of any other reason for reading this and not DNF-ing it. It sucked Donkey Kong's pixelated balls. <br/><br/>Let's go over how this sucked:<br/>1. The writing style. <br/>A)It is one of the most annoying and disjointed. Instead of the usual block paragraphs, it's a collection of one or two sentence paragraphs. It's written like a text message conversation most of the time. <br/>B) Beyond overly descriptive and not in a purple prose way. It tells step by step what the</span>
  <span id="freeText16074802044241911349" style="display:none">I think I may have encephalitis, because I can't think of any other reason for reading this and not DNF-ing it. It sucked Donkey Kong's pixelated balls. <br /><br />Let's go over how this sucked:<br />1. The writing style. <br />A)It is one of the most annoying and disjointed. Instead of the usual block paragraphs, it's a collection of one or two sentence paragraphs. It's written like a text message conversation most of the time. <br />B) Beyond overly descriptive and not in a purple prose way. It tells step by step what the character does and what everyone is wearing. If that junk was cut out it would've been 150 pages shorter. <br />2. POV. It's all first person POV, which I don't expressly hate, but it's not my preferred choice. Why it's horrible in this book is due to the inner monologue of Tina that is all a diarrhea of the brain. Most things she thinks she then says, but why do I need to read what she's going to say twice? It's a weird running stream of thought that only stops to tell you in minute detail her every action and that of everyone around her. The other POV is from Nik, but his is much less than Tina's. <br />3. Tina. This chick is TSTL and she's obscenely annoying. It's like a Furbie that snorted lines of sugary cocaine and has been set loose on the world to cause destruction. She's a very hyper character, which I detest, and the author makes her disgustingly nice to everyone...no one is that nice, it's just not realistic. She also oozes endearments to everyone, honey, darling, sweetie, with every sentence. Now between being uncontrollably saccharine, she cries, a lot. She should buy stock in Kleenex with how many boxes she must go through to sop up all her sobbing. She doesn't just cry at sad things, she cries at everything. And I've just realized I've described a two year old toddler going through the "terrible two's." Ugh. <br />4. Nik's back story. Nope, doesn't compute. It's too ridiculous. I didn't hate Nik, but his dad's connections were portrayed through rose tinted glasses. <br />5. Length and editing. Was there any? Did anyone beta read this? It needed to be severely cropped of excessiveness. It dragged down the whole book having to slog through. <br />6. Plot. The bad guy plot was pretty PG. I think I've seen better villains in Tom &amp; Jerry cartoons, at least more menacing ones. <br /><br />My only excuses for reading this are that I really like the friend zone plot lines, the synopsis sounded good and I kept waiting for it to get better, and I felt too lazy to change books. I wanted to finish this book so I could stomp it into the ground and say "HAH. That'll show you to try to annoy me into DNF-ing, I will end you." The lack of murders in this book was really disappointing. I'm going to need to read something gory now. I need dead bodies!!!!<br /><br />Alright, well, fuck this book, I'm off to eat a bag of chocolate. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16074802044241911349" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1111951592" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Srikari" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27133063-srikari"><img alt="Srikari" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Srikari" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Srikari" href="/user/show/27133063-srikari">Srikari</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27133063-srikari?shelf=sunshine-and-rainbows">sunshine-and-rainbows</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27133063-srikari?shelf=yummy-guys">yummy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27133063-srikari?shelf=kick-ass-protag">kick-ass-protag</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27133063-srikari?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1111951592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13087408154154318081"><b>EDIT[4/2/15] well I didn't like this as much as my first time. It was too too suger coated!! But I am not going to change my main review, just the rating..</b> <br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars! </b><br/>Ahh, the power of candy. Who knew it could be the beginning of something this beautiful? <br/>I actually find this really surprising, I have been reading NA books one after another and each of them ended up disappointing me more and more, but this book! Oh sweet Jesus this book! Its done something to me! It twisted my heart , playe gam</span>
  <span id="freeText13087408154154318081" style="display:none"><b>EDIT[4/2/15] well I didn't like this as much as my first time. It was too too suger coated!! But I am not going to change my main review, just the rating..</b> <br><br><b> 4.5 Stars! </b><br>Ahh, the power of candy. Who knew it could be the beginning of something this beautiful? <br>I actually find this really surprising, I have been reading NA books one after another and each of them ended up disappointing me more and more, but this book! Oh sweet Jesus this book! Its done something to me! It twisted my heart , playe games with my mind and just made me burst into rainbows at every single page!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415039520ra/11718960.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book had the depth which most NA books lack in general. It had this plot that just flowed like breeze through your hair, not completely messing it up, not just leaving it stationary. <br><br>The book was realistic. It was a fairytale without the superficial bullshit. The characters had REAL problems ,were faced with REAL dilemmas and REAL emotions. This book teaches us, life may not always be rainbows and sunshine and there might be this huge storm,but its up to u if u want to sit at home and whine or cuddle up reading your favorite book! Life is what u make it! This message was brilliantly portrayed through the characters and you a could actually feel this real connection with the book and chacharacters. <br><br><b> "Angels must have broken out in song when this man was born. I feel like breaking out in song." </b><br><br>Well I don't know if angels broke into a song, but boy I sure did!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417804474ra/12550954.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The characters are what make or break a book! Especially when it's NA. And I absolutely loved every single character. They actually did something and weren't just sitting there looking only hot and sexy. They had sexy hearts. They were people who u actually come across every day. They were the people next door! <br><br><br>And Tina! Omg! She is what I call a REAL human being ! If people like Tina actually exist in real life, well there is still hope left for humanity. She has been through ACTUAL PROBLEMS in life , (not those ones like, "omg! I lost my favorite gucci purse! My life is over") but yet she wears her heart on her sleeve, ready to accept, love and spread the joy. To you I salute!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417804474ra/12550955.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Its really nice when the characters of books inspire u this way. You feel this huge sense of satisfaction after reading! <br>It was incredible how each and every character had a quality that I admired and how each one of them gained my respect! <br><br>There is also a thin line between lust and love. And this book had love. Real love. It wasn't those books where the guy calls the girl just hot or sexy. He calls her beautiful. He calls her <b>his goofball!</b> Isn't that enough to prove how adorable this book was?<br><br>This book was a 5 star book until the end. It gained my complete admiration and love. Then why the 4.5 rating? <br> This sense of reality I had come to love of this book had slowly evaporated into BOLLYWOOD STYLE DRAMA!It got pretty clichéd with the Omar guy. I mean this shit ain't gonna happen in real life right? <br><br> I used to get so lost in this book sometimes and would laugh out so loudly that people used to think I was little lose in the head! It tickels ur funny bone, makes u think about life and touches u right in the heart! It was BEAUTIFUL piece of work! I would recommend this to everyone and anyone! <br> Best I have ever read in this genre. :')<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13087408154154318081" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14742976070109758291">4.5 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I want to protect her from everything that’s bad in the world. I want her to need me. But we’re friends. And friends don’t do shit like that.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I love, Love, LOVE friends to lover type stories, and this story is as awesome as it gets. This was so freaking cute! I had such a toothache from smiling so much. OMG, this story has everything: Strong Alpha Hero, a loveable-non-annoying heroine, a wonderful cast of supporting characters (whom I can easily see myself being friends with, too), t</span>
  <span id="freeText14742976070109758291" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I want to protect her from everything that’s bad in the world. I want her to need me. But we’re friends. And friends don’t do shit like that.</i>
</b><br /><br />I love, Love, LOVE friends to lover type stories, and this story is as awesome as it gets. This was so freaking cute! I had such a toothache from smiling so much. OMG, this story has everything: Strong Alpha Hero, a loveable-non-annoying heroine, a wonderful cast of supporting characters (whom I can easily see myself being friends with, too), tons of humor, and just the right amount of drama. So good!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“So we can be friends, right?”<br />(Wait, what?)<br />I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.<br />(Did I…? Did I just get Friend-zoned?)<br />I look over again to see Tina nodding vigorously and smiling brightly.<br />Wow, this has never happened to me before.</i>
</b><br /><br />Nik didn’t know what to do when Valentina (Tina), just waltz into his life. At first, he didn’t know if she was going to be a typical woman; only wanting him for his money and connections. He was pretty sure that’s what she wanted. Until she <i>friend-zoned</i> him. So here they were, a new friendship formed. <br /><br />Tina was all about being Nik’s friend. Yes, he’s sexy and smart, but she wasn’t ready for <i>that</i> type of relationship, yet. Being a friend to Nik would be enough for now. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> “You’re pussy whipped.”<br />I claim, “I can’t be pussy whipped. I haven’t even had the pussy to be whipped!”<br />(Take that, Ghost! Oh, wait…)<br />He chuckles, “That’s even worse, bro.”<br />(Fuck me, it totally is.) </i>
</b> <br /><br />Nik has never had a woman friend before. What is he suppose to do with her? He didn’t expect the hurricane that is Tina. All the little things she does for him completely leave him dumbfounded. Slowly, he starts to see something in Tina; something that he didn’t even know he was looking for. Suddenly, he wants to make their relationship more, but is too afraid to ruin what they currently have. Can they make the jump?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You’re it. The one. The start. The finish. <u>You</u> are how my story ends.” ~Nik </i>
</b><br /><br />OMG! Nik totally made me swoon. His slow transformation was so much fun to read, and Tina…I just loved her character. She never came off as fake or annoying. She was a breath of fresh air. Nik never stood a chance. As for the supporting characters, I LOVED each and every one of them, especially Asher (a.k.a. Ghost) and Nat. I cannot wait to read their story next!<br /></span>

  <b> Wow!!! What A Sexy Sweet Story! LOVED IT </b>
</i><br/><br/>I got exactly what I was looking for with this book.. a sweet steamy romance with very little angst, a whole lot of chemistry and steam, a little suspense, and an HEA!! The chemistry between Nik and Tina was amazing and I loved how they started out as friends--even though they were both extreamly attracted to each other from the beginning. Throw in his friends and family and her friends and this book was so much fun! I started this book late Thursday</span>
  <span id="freeText10629793938021837245" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419226ra/830903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b> Wow!!! What A Sexy Sweet Story! LOVED IT </b>
</i><br><br>I got exactly what I was looking for with this book.. a sweet steamy romance with very little angst, a whole lot of chemistry and steam, a little suspense, and an HEA!! The chemistry between Nik and Tina was amazing and I loved how they started out as friends--even though they were both extreamly attracted to each other from the beginning. Throw in his friends and family and her friends and this book was so much fun! I started this book late Thursday and stayed up until 4:30AM the next morning unable to put it down. Thank goodness I had taken a vacation day Friday or I would have been dead on my feet all day. This was that kind of story.. I just couldnt wait to experience every moment with Nik and Tina..<br><br> As completely fun as this book was there was also a lot of sadness for Tina and what horribly tragic event happend in her not to distant past that still affects her today. My heart ached so much for her and what she went through. Nik is the perfect sexy alpha man to help heal her heart.. and wow, does he heal every single inch of that girl. LOVED NIK.. that man was F-I-N-E. <br><br>Can't wait for the next book in this series!! I really like Belle Aurora's writing style..so easy to read and so funny! I laughed out loud so many times...<br><br>I highly recommend this one to anyone looking for something fun and super sexy with a touch of sadness, a dash of suspense, and a sweet HEA. <br><br><br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer746976203" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13428620814544783894"><b>4 Stars<i> (Originally Read with just a star rating 10/22/2013)</i><br/><br/>3 Stars <i>(Re-Read with review 10/17/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was great for the first half! I loved the whole development of friendship that develops into something more aspects! I just wasn’t a fan of having a gang relation to the family and stalker type situation. It felt corny and OTT. They also got a little too mushy too quickly for my tastes. I rated this 4 stars the first time I read it, but I (sadly) think I’m going to have to lo</span>
  <span id="freeText13428620814544783894" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars<i> (Originally Read with just a star rating 10/22/2013)</i><br /><br />3 Stars <i>(Re-Read with review 10/17/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was great for the first half! I loved the whole development of friendship that develops into something more aspects! I just wasn’t a fan of having a gang relation to the family and stalker type situation. It felt corny and OTT. They also got a little too mushy too quickly for my tastes. I rated this 4 stars the first time I read it, but I (sadly) think I’m going to have to lower my rating this time since my opinions on books has changed so drastically as I’ve become way pickier in my books.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Tina and Nik’s story. Tina has been admiring her work neighbor for a couple months and she decides to make a move. She isn’t interested in a relationship because of how badly she was burned in the past, so she quickly friend-zones Nik. They quickly become close friends along with her 3 friends and his 3 family members and they start a routine of spending time together regularly. There are some big secrets revealed, some past drama comes up, some sexy times, and some sad moments...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>Point Of View (POV):</b> This alternated between Tina and Nik’s POV (often switching back and forth multiple times in a chapter)<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Alright. I did start to skim in the second half because I was bored and it was too OTT for me.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, friends to love.<br /><br /><b>H (Hero) rating:</b> 4 stars. Nik. I liked him. I definitely wanted to shake him at times, but I liked him.<br /><br /><b>h (heroine) rating:</b> 4.5 stars. Tina. I really liked her. She made the book better — which says a lot because I’m usually harder on my hs!<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The both push away and also pursue the relationship at times  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW (Other Woman)/OM (Other Man) drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is an ex f-buddy of the H’s and an OM that is pursuing the h that both cause some drama for the couple  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H’s ex f-buddy causes a scene where the h thinks that the H cheats (but he doesn’t), and the h also kisses OM to play a part to protect the H — I wouldn’t consider either cheating  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated a few times shortly (most is a week), but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H was a manwhore before the h (off page), the h lost a child and her mother in an accident (off page), and kidnapping/criminal activity/violence/murder (on page)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This ends with a HEA ending but I’m greedy and I still would’ve liked more because of the way it was quickly wrapped up right after the conflict was resolved <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they’re married and she just had their baby <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating (see above)<br />- <b>Does Not</b>
