<div id="review_731409507" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/731409507" />
    <a title="Shay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24105480-shay"><img alt="Shay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380043271p2/24105480.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/731409507?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shay" href="/user/show/24105480-shay">Shay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24105480-shay?shelf=never-read-again">never-read-again</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer731409507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4878400027858034723">First, I don't think I've ever disagreed more strongly with my book friends than I do about this book!! I also feel that if anyone gives a 1 or 2 star rating, it deserves an explanation. Especially since I've read some of Belle's other work and really loved it!! And I will continue to read her books, I just really didn't like this one and there are several reasons.<br/><br/>1. Too many grammatical errors. This reads like unedited fan fiction. ("date rate drug", "we're" instead of "were", there were others</span>
  <span id="freeText4878400027858034723" style="display:none">First, I don't think I've ever disagreed more strongly with my book friends than I do about this book!! I also feel that if anyone gives a 1 or 2 star rating, it deserves an explanation. Especially since I've read some of Belle's other work and really loved it!! And I will continue to read her books, I just really didn't like this one and there are several reasons.<br /><br />1. Too many grammatical errors. This reads like unedited fan fiction. ("date rate drug", "we're" instead of "were", there were others but you get my point.) It reminded me of those papers I would crank out at the last minute and turn in without re-reading.<br /><br />2. Unrealistic setting. I love New York. I LOVE LOVE LOVE when books are set in NYC because there are so many places and settings for the characters. But I didn't buy that this was set in NY for one minute and here's why.<br /> A. Tina has a piece of shit car that barely runs. So how can she afford a two bedroom apartment? It's clear in the story that she hasn't touched the "other money" and that she is living off of Safira profit. Not only does she have a 2br apartment but she has to pay to park said piece of shit car. I tried to justify it by saying maybe she lives in Brooklyn or The Bronx or even Queens. But I couldn't really ever convince myself that was the case. <br /> B. The White Rabbit and Safira sound like Manhattan businesses. And there is street parking in front of Safira. Yep, that can happen but not all-day parking.<br /> C. And THEN there is Nik's place. There is no way a sprawling 9br(??) gated house is on Manhattan. It's sure as shit not in The Bronx. It would have made more sense for him to live in Jersey. Or Connecticut. Details matter and this bugged me from the get-go. If the setting was upstate NY or another city, she should have said-so. This setting read like suburbia with the local coffee shop and clerks that remember your name.<br /><br />3. Lazy storytelling. As you can see, I love details. The best part of reading a book is developing the scene and characters in your mind and then "watching" them in action. It's how I become emotionally invested in a book. Early on, Lola says, "...So I reach over to my groceries, open a can of chopped tomatoes and dump em on her head!" Um...what? Did you have a can opener in your purse? Did you really open a CAN of tomatoes right there in the check out line? I made myself laugh picturing this absurd scene. Plus, who does that? Later, in the club, the girls have all slid into a "large booth" in the VIP lounge. The guys then show up and slide in with them. When the She-devil shows up, all of a sudden, all four girls are in her face. ?? WTF? Did they teleport? Because I've never exited a booth without sliding out and if someone has slid in next to me, they are going to have to move first. This probably wouldn't have bothered me so much except I couldn't stop thinking about the goddamn tomatoes!!! <br /><br />4. Weird timeline of events and unrealistic character interaction. When Tina's dad showed up, I expected some sort of heartfelt moment due to the different ways they were forced to grieve their losses. But alas, we get the cheesiest scene in the whole book:<br /><br />Dad: OMG, your douchy ex-boyfriend called and instead of calling you, I jumped on a flight from Cali because it's such a quick flight and super easy to get here. Cheap, too.<br /><br />Tina: OMG, Daddy, it's OK, Nik's here. Oh, hi Jace.<br /><br />Jace: Huh huh, you look good.<br /><br />Nik: He wants your money.<br /><br />Tina: *gasp* No! <br /><br />Jace: OK, I'll go now.<br /><br />Nik: Don't worry Tina's Dad, I'm here now.<br /><br />Dad: Ok, I'll just go jump back on a plane to Cali instead of spending some time with my daughter that I haven't seen in a long time. Ciao!<br /><br />I gave myself a migraine from all the eye-rolling and skimmed the rest of the book. Oh, and I can't even talk about Omarr. This was turning into Gangs of New York meets Gossip Girl and I wasn't buying any of it.<br /><br />Later, Nik tries to find Jace but he's already back in California. (The shuttle service from LaGuardia to LAX is pretty awesome. SMH) That whole interaction seemed forced and completely unnecessary. Tina had already gotten over Jace, there was no reason to bring him in for 30 seconds of dialogue. So dumb.<br /><br />As I said, I will read the next book and will continue to read Belle's work. But this fell flat for me.<br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="4878400027858034723" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10677369603267606269" style="display:none"><b>Friend-Zoned is the very cute story of Tina and Nik. Tina has been in been in New York for the past couple of years. I found their interactions both humorous and sweet. There were a few over the top moments but overall it worked. I enjoyed that the book was written from a dual POV. <div id="review_623415056" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/623415056" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/623415056?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer623415056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7331325144237801052">3.5 Stars<br/><br/><u>
  <b>The Good:</b>
</u><br/>I loved the author's voice. She has that casual writing style (a la Kristen Ashley) that makes you feel like you're a part of the action, best friends with the girls, and either lusting after the men or wanting them to just be in your vicinity to protect you. The women are quirky as hell, each of them with their own set of wacky one liners and silly idiosyncrasies. It's easy to relate to them, because they actually seem like real people. <br/><br/>Tina owns a clothing boutique and lo</span>
  <span id="freeText7331325144237801052" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br /><br /><u>
  <b>The Good:</b>
</u><br />I loved the author's voice. She has that casual writing style (a la Kristen Ashley) that makes you feel like you're a part of the action, best friends with the girls, and either lusting after the men or wanting them to just be in your vicinity to protect you. The women are quirky as hell, each of them with their own set of wacky one liners and silly idiosyncrasies. It's easy to relate to them, because they actually seem like real people. <br /><br />Tina owns a clothing boutique and loves to dress pretty, but she's not over the top annoying, and she realizes and expresses that two hundred dollars for a jacket is outrageous. I hate it when a book talks about spending money like a rich person when their lead female is an obvious middle class American. Tina is down to earth and extremely loyal. Nik lives a life that seems great to him...a string of gorgeous women to sleep with but never stay with and a hip club that keeps him rich. He's also loyal to his family and friends and feels responsible for those around him. His reaction to Tina at first is confusion...this bubbly, cute chick sends him candy kisses and tells him to smile?! What is that all about? When she Friend Zones him, he's even more confused at his reaction to her. It's as if she threw down the gauntlet and suddenly, he feels challenged.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Tina must be a fairy or some shit. I've never been affectionate. In fact, the thought of being affectionate used to make me sneer. But it's different with her. Most women who hug or rub up against me in public want to be seen with me or want something from me. Tina, though, you can see it in her face when she hugs you, it's genuine. It's her emotions bieng put out there on display and she doesn't care who sees."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>The Bad:</b>
</u><br /><br />Sometime after the 60% mark, Tina turns all girlie and giggly and cries an awful lot. I get tired of the word "giggle" fairly quickly. And even though the thing that I originally loved about Tina was her cute-ness, the cute wore off after awhile and she started to seem airheaded and weepy. The girl cried buckets!!! <br /><br />Overall, this was a fun, sexy little romance that mostly engaged me throughout the entire story. I'm very much looking forward to Ghost and Natalie's story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7331325144237801052" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Each were unique &amp; individual . The girls were funny &amp; sassy .... They were like a mix between watching a friends tv show &amp; kristen Ashley's rock chicks !!!<br />I WANT TO BE IN THEIR CLICK !!!<br /> <br />The guys ......ohhhh the guuuyysss !!!! <br />HOT !!! That's the 1st word I MUST USE LOL <br />They were all plagued with heart break in different ways , all bad-boy beautiful .......&amp; did I mention HAWT !!! <br /><br />Together they make a beautiful band of misfits that fit together PERFECTLY !!! <br /><br />This book made me giggle &amp; snort laughing :) <br />It made me swoon &amp; .... Ummm ... Wiggle in my seat over some of the ....shall we say "adult moments" ;) <br />BUT it also made me cry !!<br />Don't judge me !!!! <br />There was a piano &amp; singing involved !!!<br />&amp; don't even get me started on the crunchy peanut butter cupcake thing !!!<br />( u will know what I mean WHEN u read this book ! ) <br /><br />I have read sooooo many books lately that are full of so much angst &amp; sadness &amp; drama ....although I do LUV that , I think that is what made this book soooooo bloody refreshing !!! <br />This book is about beautiful people &amp; wonderful friendships &amp; a love story that just made me want to grab some Pom poms &amp; do a happy dance !!! <br /><br />THANKU BELLA AURORA for giving me a book buzz that will last a year !!! <br /><br />U left me feeling nothing but satisfaction !!!<br />For this I bow down my fangirl head to u :) <br /><br />Now stop reading my review &amp; GO BUY THIS BOOK !!!! Lol </span>
  <a data-text-id="9588291398133374679" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2442906773?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨Skye✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨Skye✨" href="/user/show/30014834-skye">✨Skye✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22616939-friend-zoned">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30014834-skye?shelf=3-star-was-okay">3-star-was-okay</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2442906773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9907339751377657334">Awww. This was just the light-hearted, fun, feel good read I wanted. It's entirely unrealistic and a little juvenile, but it was just such a joy to read!<br/>Friend-Zoned, much as the title suggests, follows two people who have defined each other as friends. Tina is the manager of a clothing store and has a tragic past. Nik owns a successful nightclub across the street from Tina's clothing store and has his own baggage to carry. This was one of the cutest romances I've read for a long time and I just</span>
  <span id="freeText9907339751377657334" style="display:none">Awww. This was just the light-hearted, fun, feel good read I wanted. It's entirely unrealistic and a little juvenile, but it was just such a joy to read!<br />Friend-Zoned, much as the title suggests, follows two people who have defined each other as friends. Tina is the manager of a clothing store and has a tragic past. Nik owns a successful nightclub across the street from Tina's clothing store and has his own baggage to carry. This was one of the cutest romances I've read for a long time and I just rooted for these two so much! Their relationship was sexy and sweet and I just loved them together.<br />The characters in this were fantastic. I loved the little family they created and how everyone got along so well. Ghost and Nat are my new power ship and I can't wait to read the sequel to this that I believe is focussed around them! CeeCee was so adorable, Max is such a doting father and I just loved the dynamics of this group together.<br />The plot itself was great, or at least for the vast majority. I really enjoyed the scenarios that Tina and Nik found themself in as they fell in love, how they met, how they gradually began seeing each other more and more. One of my main issues with the book was the inclusion of some plot lines that id din't feel were necessary or fit into the story very well-<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the Omarr and gang stuff felt very out of place and I don't think it was required. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Aside from that plot issue, I do have another negative, and that is the treatment of an ex-lover of Nik's. Is she a nice person? No, and she does her best to split Nik and Tina up, but nobody deserves to be slut shamed and there was one incident which I thought was VERY out of character (<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Nik actually assaults Sissy, and almost strangles her. This was not okay in any way and just completely did not fit with how respectful and sweet Nik was up to this point. If I based my review on this fact, it would get a 1 star, but I do think this was just such a short section of the book and I chose to imagine the book without this in it. However, it does need to be acknowledged as a major issue.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)</span>
  <a data-text-id="9907339751377657334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_742648367" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/742648367" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/742648367?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer742648367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6665052544371954406">I love a good friends-to-lovers story, but I suspect I may be too cynical for such a sweet book. While I really liked the premise, and the way that the story played out, I found the heroine irritatingly sweet and thought parts of it were really corny. <br/><br/>Tina sees the best in everybody, she wants to help everybody, she’s affectionate, and loving, and sees the bright side of every situation. Yeah, these are good qualities to have, but it was just a bit much for me. She was so annoyingly perfect, and</span>
  <span id="freeText6665052544371954406" style="display:none">I love a good friends-to-lovers story, but I suspect I may be too cynical for such a sweet book. While I really liked the premise, and the way that the story played out, I found the heroine irritatingly sweet and thought parts of it were really corny. <br /><br />Tina sees the best in everybody, she wants to help everybody, she’s affectionate, and loving, and sees the bright side of every situation. Yeah, these are good qualities to have, but it was just a bit much for me. She was so annoyingly perfect, and everybody instantly adored her. It’s irritating, and I found I couldn’t take her seriously. But again, that’s just me and my clearly pessimistic opinion.<br /><br />Tina owns a clothing store, and has often noticed the guy working at a nightclub across the street from her shop. He’s smoking hot, but always looks so serious. So in one of her good samaritan moves, she sends him some candy with a note to try and make him smile. <br /><br />Nik is the Owner / Manager of the White Rabbit nightclub. He has been taken advantage of by women in the past – trying to trap him or just wanting him for his money - so is understandably very wary of Tina’s gesture. <br /><br /><blockquote><i>“I don’t have relationships or girlfriends. I have fuck buddies. Because I fuck. Often. I most definitely </i>don’t<i> make love. I might not screw hard all the time but even slow screwing is just screwing.”</i></blockquote><br />He has Tina escorted over to his office so that he can figure out her motives and he gets the shock of his life when he meets beautiful, big-hearted woman, and discovers that she's actually geniuine. Figuring she wants a relationship with him, he is getting to let her down gently when she comes out with this…<br /><br /><blockquote><i>“So we can be friends, right?”</i><br />Wait, what?<br /><i>I stare at her, a frown forming at my mouth.</i><br />Did I..? Did I just get Friend-zoned?</blockquote><br />What follows is a rapidly moving, quickly deepening friendship where Tina burrows her way into every facet of Nik’s life. She bakes for him and his boys, she invites him to lunch, she gives him hugs, and he surprisingly finds himself enjoying spending time with her. Pretty soon his boys and her girls are completely intertwined, hanging out, having fun, hooking up, and becoming somewhat of a family. It’s really sweet, but again I found bits of it to be cheesy (the guys teasing each other and calling each other "knucklehead", excessive amounts of giggling and sing-alongs around the piano… really?). <br /><br />Things started to pick up for me when Tina and Nik realise that they are wildly attracted to each other.<br /><br /><blockquote><i>10:16am<br />Thinking about Tina.<br />11:04am<br />Thinking about Tina’s perfect ass.<br />12:37pm<br />Thinking about Tina panting under me in bed.<br />1:02pm<br />Going to the bathroom to jerk off.<br /><br />I walk back into my office after finally getting some much needed relief.<br /></i>Not hard anymore, are you?! Take that, penis!</blockquote><br />It’s a beautifully natural progression from friends to more, and even though there are a few false starts, their feelings for each other just continue to grow, and I was cheering as things finally started to happen. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You and me, Tina. It’s gonna happen … Mark my words, baby.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Tina’s background is truly devastating. She has been through hell, and is still recovering from a horrific trauma in her past. I understood her feelings about entering a new relationship, but I loved how brave she was, and how she was able to move forward from all that she had suffered. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I don’t know how much is left of my heart to break but I know enough to say next time would destroy me. Right now I’m bent, not broken. Next time will break me. I don’t need a perfect relationship. I just need someone who won’t give up on me.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Nik has never had a relationship before, and I loved watching him realise his feelings as he falls and falls hard for Tina. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Never met anyone like her in my life. So giving with her heart. I’ll do anything to protect that heart. I want it to be mine to protect.”</i>
</blockquote><br />And oh, holy hotness! Belle Aurora writes a great love scene, and there is plenty of steaminess in this book! Nik is clearly talented, and I liked that Tina was able to let loose and show a bit of a teasing side when she and Nik were together. <br /><br />But along with the burgeoning relationship, Nik has some darkness in his past that comes back to wreak havoc in his future, and I liked this part of the story. It brings some depth, and provides the opportunity for some badassery which I really enjoyed. <br /><br />But it’s all about the romance, and I loved that. Nik is so full of swoon, and the two of them are so in love, completely accepting of each other and absolutely there for each other, and I loved them together. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re it. The one. The start. The finish. You are how my story ends.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I also liked the big group of characters. This is a really close bunch and there is a bit of detail given about ‘the boys’ and ‘the girls’, and I feel like I know some of them well already. The set up is already beginning for their relationships, and I’m excited to go on with the series and read their stories. <br /><br />So many people love this series, and I can absolutely see the appeal. The sweetness and cheese was almost too much for me in the beginning, and I considered putting it down, but it was the fact that so many people adore these books, and the promise of the romance to come that kept me going. And I’m glad I did. I really enjoyed the love story aspect of the book, and although both Tina and Nik had moments of stupid, it was resolved well, and they got their HEA which was again really cheesy, but it still left me smiling. <br /><br />3 stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6665052544371954406" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_656248245" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656248245" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/656248245?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-contemporary-romance">genre-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=funny-funny-har-har">funny-funny-har-har</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-i-wanna-hug">hero-i-wanna-hug</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-hot-male-in-my-harem">hero-hot-male-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=best-of-the-best-2013">best-of-the-best-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-perfect-man-syndrome">hero-perfect-man-syndrome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=sweeter-than-honey">sweeter-than-honey</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer656248245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12279839508735368729"><b>Review @ <a href='' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/>Valentina Tomic, Tina to her friends, has watched the unbelievably hunky man who works across the street from her shop come out for his break three times a day, not once has he cracked a smile. She decides to try and brighten up his day. She never knew that some sweets and a note would lead to her actually becoming friends with him, even if what she starts to feel for him does starts to bat him out the friend zone. <br/><br/>I got this book on the off chance, I felt like taking a </span>
  <span id="freeText12279839508735368729" style="display:none"><b>Review @ <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br />Valentina Tomic, Tina to her friends, has watched the unbelievably hunky man who works across the street from her shop come out for his break three times a day, not once has he cracked a smile. She decides to try and brighten up his day. She never knew that some sweets and a note would lead to her actually becoming friends with him, even if what she starts to feel for him does starts to bat him out the friend zone. <br /><br />I got this book on the off chance, I felt like taking a gamble and trying out an author I hadn't read before. And I really liked the cover. I am immensely pleased with myself that I took that chance! I loved this book, it was funny, sexy and incredible sweet without being nauseating. Friend-zoned is essentially about two unlikely people meeting and becoming friends but then trying to get the transition from friends to much more, maybe not an original story line but that didn't stop me from enjoying the hell out of this book. <br /><br />The relationship between Nik and Tina was incredibly sweet, I loved how close they became, the connection between them really shone out the pages and the sexual tension seemed to build up naturally till I was dying for them to just rip each others clothes off and get their freak on. But, as well as a lovable central couple Friend-zoned also built up a great group of secondary characters, Nik and Tina's friends, and the whole group meshed really well together and I can't wait to read more about each of one them. <br /><br />The humour in this book also stood out for me, if you are a Tara Sivec or R.L. Mathewson fan, then I reckon you will love this, they all have sarcastic bantering humour that I certainly know I love. The only part of the book that felt odd to me was some random gangster stuff that gets thrown in in the middle of the book. It was either completely unrealistic or mobsters are a lot friendlier than the modern age gives them credit for. But even a few random mob guys couldn't dampen my enjoyment of this book. <br /><br />This was a fantastic read, light, funny but with an emotional punch and characters that connected not just with their HEA but displayed a whole host of different types of relationships. I have now found a new author for me to follow, as I definitely plan on getting whatever Ms Aurora brings out next.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12279839508735368729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pxFLziEsksodu062rJf6f43DHqznoO1qnTvYZQIWm6dqalZgRhYhBUUduokxWVMrjDzgLDqBKwcXldp461mcWA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U2xH8V9WeXtbV+EuC7JoUxI/IRXdaZzVIp/MS57of7OeF1pfOGzKtAPxFRGWfMEHE8DflQBIWrioMc5Wd6d4TA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15070505130197464758">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br/>At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home.   <span id="freeText15070505130197464758" style="display:none">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br />At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home. She stumbled across Sandra Brown’s Breath of Scandal and fell in love with romance.<br />Having been brought up in a loud and boisterous family of Croatian descent, she developed a natural love for dramatics and laughter. Only some years ago had she discovered a new love. <br />Humorous romance novels.<br />So many authors had opened a brand new world where she could lose herself yet feel safe and at home in their stories. Belle has been known to become a screeching banshee while anxiously awaiting their newest titles.<br />Belle never thought she would write. It had never interested her until recently. Friend-Zoned began to form and in February this year Belle typed the words Chapter One. And she fell in love.<br />With words.<br />With writing.<br />With a creative imagination she never knew she harbored.<br /><br />Belle Aurora is a USA Today best-selling author.</span>

          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
